		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != '5e24ba00a2821c697c38405e52ff2eded1d44bdb') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}

	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '5e24ba00a2821c697c38405e52ff2eded1d44bdb') {

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '5e24ba00a2821c697c38405e52ff2eded1d44bdb') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/oidplus_base.css');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/oidplus_base.css');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/oidplus_base.css')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/oidplus_base.css', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/oidplus_base.css') !== '2020c9dee98b99fcf461895cc590b4f456db20a8') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/oidplus_base.css');
		}
	}
}

		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/aid/OIDplusAid.css') !== '06ce4e287b625d407c5fd8e7703eb0c98a21bb2d') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/aid/OIDplusAid.css');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/aid/OIDplusAid.css');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/aid/OIDplusAid.css')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/aid/OIDplusAid.css', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/aid/OIDplusAid.css') !== '9f956d67680c53463f144cc97101611b9020f773') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/aid/OIDplusAid.css');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('.version.php', "<?php // Revision 1401\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('.version.php')) !== '<?php // Revision 1401') err('Could not write to .version.php!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
